–Ø —É–±—Ä–∞–ª–∞ —É —Å–µ–±—è –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–π–Ω–µ—Ä
(celebrity)

There are people who we admire and can only dream of being close to them. If I had an opportunity to catch someone from the shiny streets of Hollywood and stick that person to me, that probably would be Daniel Radcliffe. Let me be positive that this can actually happen!

First of all, he is a symbol of my childhood because being a little girl I would spend evenings immersed in reading books about Harry Potter, dreaming about meeting that boy from the self-titled movie.

Secondly, Daniel or Dan, as he was called in a Fellon TV show, where he could unleash his potential in rap reading and show the whole world his vast range of abilities, it looked like he was in his elements. So, he does not seem to be going for the easy way!

Additional, Radcliffe is a typical English young man with that captivating accent. My probable relationship with him could work out beneficially so that I move to London, the place which is worthy of visiting and living in.

To sum up, this is an absolutely hypothetical situation and generally, I do not set unrealistic goals, however, future with Daniel seems so appealing that I can start booking a one-way ticket to London.

–ö—Ä–æ–º–µ –Ω–∏—Ö –æ–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª–∏—Ç—å –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å PointSerialize —Å –¥–≤—É–º—è –Ω–µ—Å—Ç–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–º–∏ –º–µ—Ç–æ–¥–∞–º–∏: –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π –∏–∑ –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã—Ö –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è–µ—Ç –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—å –≤ –∑–∞–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–æ–º —Ñ–∞–π–ª —Å–µ—Ä–∏–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –æ–±—ä–µ–∫—Ç–∞ —Ç–∏–ø–∞ Point; –≤—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–π ‚Äì –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è–µ—Ç —á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏–∑ –∑–∞–¥–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–æ–º —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞ –∏ –¥–µ—Å–µ—Ä–∏–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—é –æ–±—ä–µ–∫—Ç–∞ —Ç–∏–ø–∞ Point.

/**
     * Separates the given expration into tokens by a space character
     * @param expr is a string with operands and operations, separated by a space
     * @return
     */
     std::list<std::string> separatedTokens(std::string &expr)
    {
        std::list<std::string> tokens;
        std::string::iterator it=expr.begin();
        std::string substring;
        for(it;it!=expr.end();)
        {
            while (*it != ' ' && it != expr.end())
            {
                const char symb = *it;
                substring.push_back(symb);
                ++it;
            }
            tokens.push_back(substring.substr(0,substring.length()));
            substring.clear();
            if (it != expr.end())
            {
                ++it;
            }
        }
        return tokens;
    }

              switch (op->getArity())

/* –ó–ê–î–ê–ù–ò–ï:

  –ù–∞–∑–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ: –ø–æ–¥–º–Ω–æ–∂–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ —è–∑—ã–∫–∞ D
  –û–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä—ã: +, -, *, /, =, >, <, >=, <=, ++, |, &, %. writeln()
  –°–ª–æ–∂–Ω—ã–µ –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä—ã(—Ñ–∏—á–∏): struct, –æ–±—Ä–∞—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∫ –ø–æ–ª—è–º —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—ã
  –¢–∏–ø—ã: int, bool, string
  –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä –∫–æ–¥–∞:

  struct Point
  {
  int x,y;
  }
  int k = 0;
  int m = 4;
  Point p;
  p.x = k;
  p.y = m;
  writeln(p.x);
  writeln(p.y);

  –û–∂–∏–¥–∞–µ–º—ã–π –≤—ã–≤–æ–¥:
  0
  4

  –°–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∫–∞: http://dlang.org/

  */

grammar MyLittleGrammar;

options
{
  language = CSharp;
}

@header{
  using System;
  using System.Collections;
}

@members{
  Hashtable memory = new Hashtable();
}

@parser::namespace { Generated }
@lexer::namespace  { Generated }

 startrule          : (struct_declaration|function_declaration|sentence)* main_program?
                                            (sentence|struct_declaration|function_declaration)* ;

 main_program       : type 'main' function_params_declaration function_body;

expr : LBRAC expr RBRAC
       |'-' expr
       |expr (MULT|DEV) expr
       |expr (PLUS|MINUS) expr
       |expr AND expr
       |expr OR expr
       |VALINT
       |VALBOOL
       |ID
       ;
expr : LBRAC expr RBRAC # Parenthesis
       |'-' expr #Pos_neg
       |expr (MULT|DEV|MOD) expr  #Multiply_Divide
       |expr (PLUS|MINUS) expr     #Add_Subtract
       |expr (LE | LT| GE | GT) expr # Comparisons
       |expr AND expr # Log_and
       |expr OR expr # Log_or
       |VALINT     # Int
       |VALBOOL  # Double
       |VALSTRING     # String
       |ID #Idd
       ;

        bracket_expr        :left_value* bracket right_value*;
        operation            : AROPERATIONS|LOPERATIONS|BOOPERATIONS;

        right_value          : operation expr;
        left_value           : expr operation;
        bracket              : LBRAC expr RBRAC;

 sentence           : type variable (ASSIGN (expr|bracket_expr))? (COMMA variable (ASSIGN (bracket_expr|expr))?)* SEMICOL #variable_declaration
                     |id ASSIGN expr SEMICOL #assign_expression
                     |function_id function_params SEMICOL #function_call
                     |expr INCRDECR SEMICOL #incr_decr_statement
                     |SEMICOL+ #empty_operator
                     ;



 value               : (VALINT|int_id) ((LOPERATIONS|AROPERATIONS|BOOPERATIONS) (DIGIT+|'(' '-' (DIGIT+|int_id)')')|int_id)* #int_expression
                    | (VALSTRING|string_id) ((LOPERATIONS|AROPERATIONS|BOOPERATIONS) (VALSTRING|string_id))* #string_expression
                    | (VALBOOL|bool_id) ((LOPERATIONS|BOOPERATIONS) (VALBOOL|bool_id))* #bool_expression
                    | value INCRDECR #var
                    | id #var
                    ;



 struct_declaration   : STRUCT struct_id struct_body;
 struct_body          : LCURLB sentence* RCURLB;
 struct_id            : ID;
 struct_pole          : object DOT field;
 object               : ID;
 field                : ID;

 //For functions
 function_declaration        : type function_id function_params_declaration function_body;
 function_body               : LCURLB sentence* RCURLB;
 function_id                 : ID;
 function_params_declaration : LBRAC (type param_id (COMMA type param_id)*)? RBRAC;
 param_id                    : ID;

 function_params             : LBRAC (expr (COMMA expr)*)? RBRAC;

 //Different id types
 variable                    : ID;
 int_id                      : ID|struct_pole;
 string_id                   : ID|struct_pole;
 bool_id                     : ID|struct_pole;
 id                          : MINUS? ID|struct_pole;
 type                   : STRING
                        |INT
                        |BOOLEAN
                        |ID
                        ;

//Values


// Operators
 AROPERATIONS         : '+'|'-'|'*'|'/'|'%';
 LOPERATIONS          : '>'|'<'|'<='|'>='|'=='|'!=';
 BOOPERATIONS         : '&'| '|';
 INCRDECR             : '--' | '++';

 TRUE                 : 'true';
 FALSE                : 'false';
 VALBOOL              : TRUE|FALSE;

int *backwards(int n){
    srand(time(0));
    int *arr=new int[n];
    for(int i=10,j=0;j<n && i>=0;++j){
        int r=rand();
        arr[j]=i;
        if(r%2==0){
            ‚Äîi;
        }
    }
    return arr;
}
